# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Caliper Containment Algorithm ^cb9zyI0m

Thicket Algorithm:
    Read in cali file as normal
    Read in trace file
    Read in remarks file
    Initialzie node stack

    Traverse trace and thicket graph:
        Associate entries with nodes in thicket

    Traverse trace and process remarks
        IF within range of existing node
            Add to node data ^JWmDDYl9
